In 2022, Glenmede ("GM") adopted a change in accounting principle related to its defined benefit retirement plans. Upon adoption, GM recorded a cumulative effect adjustment that decreased beginning equity on 1/1/22 by $2.7 miliion. At the end of the 2022 audit, GM's auditors determined that there should not have been a net impact to equity. GM recorded the adjustment after the final filing of GM's Q4 '22 Call Report. GM management communcated with GM's lead OCC examiner regarding the matter and refiling was not deemed necessary by the OCC. The adjustment to equity in 2023 reflects the reversal of the $2.7 million net reduction in equity in 2022.	Adjustment to PY change in accounting principle
